(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

    (at ?loc - location)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

 (define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )
  
  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (visited ?to))
  )
)

(define (problem explore-house-p16)
  (:domain house-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry bathroom laundry-room corridor - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at laundry-room)
    (visited kitchen)
    (visited pantry)
    (visited bathroom)
    (visited laundry-room)
    (door kitchen pantry north)
    (door pantry kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen pantry)
    (door-open pantry kitchen)
    (door kitchen bathroom south)
    (door bathroom kitchen north)
    (door-open kitchen bathroom)
    (door-open bathroom kitchen)
    (door bathroom laundry-room west)
    (door laundry-room bathroom east)
    (door-open bathroom laundry-room)
    (door-open laundry-room bathroom)
    (door kitchen corridor east)
    (door corridor kitchen west)
    (door-closed kitchen corridor)
    (door-closed corridor kitchen)
  )
  (:goal
    (and
      (at laundry-room)
      (not (visited corridor))
    )
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (visited ?to))
  )
)

  (:domain house-exploration)
  (:objects
    kitchen pantry bathroom laundry-room corridor - location
    north south east west - direction
  )
  (:init
    (at kitchen)
    (visited kitchen)
    (visited pantry)
    (visited bathroom)
    (visited laundry-room)
    (door kitchen pantry north)
    (door pantry kitchen south)
    (door-open kitchen pantry)

    (door kitchen bathroom south)
    (door bathroom kitchen north)

    (door-open laundry-room bathroom)
    (door kitchen corridor east)
    (door corridor kitchen west)
    (door-closed kitchen corridor)
    (door-closed corridor kitchen)
  )
  (:goal
    (and
      (not (visited corridor))
    )
  )
)

    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (visited ?to))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain house-exploration)
  (:requirements :strips :typing)
  (:types location direction)

  (:predicates
    (at ?loc - location)
    (door ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    (door-open ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (door-closed ?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location)
    (visited ?loc - location)
  )

  (:action open-door
    :parameters (?loc1 - location ?loc2 - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?loc1) (door ?loc1 ?loc2 ?dir) (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2))
    :effect (and (door-open ?loc1 ?loc2) (not (door-closed ?loc1 ?loc2)))
  )

  (:action move
    :parameters (?from - location ?to - location ?dir - direction)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (door ?from ?to ?dir) (door-open ?from ?to))
    :effect (and (at ?to) (not (at ?from)) (visited ?to))
  )
)
